 apane is daure ke pehle din pradhanmantri modi ne british pradhanmantridavid camran ke saath dwipaksheeya vaartaki or kai samjhauton par hastakshar bhi hue
 The Prime Minister addressed the Parliament of Britain
 aisa karne vaale ve pehle bhartiya pradhanmantri hai
 Let's see what India got from this visit of Prime Minister? 1
 UNSC main daavedaari kaa joardaar samarthanbritain ne sanyukt raashtra suraksha parishad main bharat kii sthaayee sadsyta kii daavedaari kaa samarthan kiya
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi thanked Cameron for his strong support at the joint press conference
 british pradhanmantri david camran ne kaha ki sabase purana va sabase bada loktantr bharat va britain swaabhaavik saajhedaar hai
 2
 asainya parmaanu samjhaute par hastakshrapradhanmantri narendra modi ke teen divasiy britain daure ke pehle din donon pakshon dwaara pratinidhimandal stareey vaarta ke baad bharat va britain ne ek asainya parmaanu samjhaute par hastakshar kiye
 Issuing a shared statement with the British Prime Minister David Cameron after the talks, PM Modi said, 'today we signed a civil nuclear deal
 yah hamaare parsparik vishwaas kaa pratik he
 '3
 smart city pariyojna main sathdonon netaaon ne britain va bharat ke bich aarthik, raksha va vaishvik saajhedaari ko majboot karne kii patibaddhta jataai
 At the same time, Cameron announced that Britain will cooperate in making Amravati, Indore and Pune a smart city
 4
 Nine billion pounds agreement During Prime Minister Narendra Modi's first UK visit, there were nine billion pound agreements between India and Britain, of which six are very important
 isamen doorsanchaar, saura urja, nivesh, svachh urja, healthcare, stock exange, antariksh kshetra samet tamaam kshetron main sahyog kii baat shaamil he
 Describing Britain as the third largest investor in India, PM Modi said that India has invested more in the UK than the total investment in the European Union
 5
 Initiatives to seize Dawood's property India also handed over a dossier to Britain as part of its efforts to clamp down on India's enemies
 jisamen most wanted apradhi or pakistan main sharan paaedaud ibrahim ke britain main thikaanon ko sij karne kii maangashamil he
 These documents contain details of Dawood's properties in Britain
 pravartan nideshaalay ke mutabik, duniya kii 10 deshon main daaud kii 50 prime property hai
 Their value is estimated at around Rs 3000 crore
 lekin sabase zyada nivesh britain or landan main hi hua he
 Dawood and his close associates have 15 properties in the UK, valued at around Rs 1500 crore
 6
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi tried his best to woo the investors of Britain during his address at London's Gild Hall
 landan ke aitihaasik gildhaul main vyapaar jagat kii badi shakhsiyaton ko sambodhit karte hue modi ne kaha ki bhartiya arthvyavastha kii tarakkee ke liye 'jaruri halaat' paidaa kiye gaye hai
 He also said that it is sensible to join India
 'landan main british pradhanmantri david camran ke saath saajha bayaan ke dauraan piem narendra modi ne ashishnutaa ke sawaal par chuppi todi
 The PM said that India is the land of Gandhi and Buddha and India does not accept any such thing
 unhone kaha, 'desh ke kisi bhi kone main hui har ghatana hamaare liye gambhir he
 The law will work strictly
 har naagarik ke vichaar kii raksha karnaa hamaari jimmedaari he
 ' mohali menmphunjab School Education Board ke head offis main huipress conference main 12veen ke riselt (12th Result) kii ghoshnaa hui

 lekin PSEB board ne merit list jari kar toppers ke naamon kii ghoshnaa kar di

 ek baar phir bhartiya janata party ke andar pradhanmantri pad kii daavedaari ko lekar chal rahi khinchataan ko tool mil gaya he

 bihar bijepi adhyaksh ne modi kaa gungan karte hue kaha he ki agar modi aagaamee gujarat vidhansabha chunaav main hetric lagaate hai to piem ke liye unki daavedaari or majboot hogi

 iske alaava unhone yah bhi kaha ki hamaari party badi he, uske baad gathbandhan aata he

 gauratlab he ki narendra modi philhal chunaavon main vyast hai or chunavi bhaashanon ke dauraan akasar hi centre kii upie sarkaar par nishaanaa sadhate rahete hai

 film 'jajba' ke pramotion event ke dauraan aishwarya raay kaa peechha karne vaale phans ke chalate aishwarya raay kii security badha di gai he
 Actually this decision was taken when Aishwarya recently attended a wrap up party for her film 'jazbaa' at a nightclub in Mumbai
 aishwarya raay is party main kaaphi der se pahunchi lekin apni chahetistarako dekhne ke liye unke phans kaa tantaa lag gaya
 Aishwarya had reached this party with her two security officers but people were seen outside the club to see her
 phans kii bheed ko hataane ke liye club ke bounsars or security officers ko bahut mashkkat hui or aishwarya ko club se baahar nikaalnaa behad mushakil ho gaya
 a source associated with the promotion of 'jazbaa' film told, 'we have been seeing for some time that many incidents have happened with the stars due to the fans, so we do not want to take any chance with Aishwarya so that she will not have any chance during the promotion Also faced problems

 kya desh ko yah jaanane kii jarurat nahin he?
 He said, will the countrymen not ask for an answer on this? i do not want to speak in political language, but i want to say that corruption is the most important issue before the country
 
 
 
 This is the pain, and anguish of our country
 modi ne kaha, puraane jamaane ke televijan dharawahikon main bhai bhatijawad bhrashtachar kii mukhya vajah hota tha
 
 
 This has changed over time
 
 
 bhrashtachar par mamaa or bhaanje kaa nayaa dharawahik aayaa or ab yah saas, bahu or damaad ke serial main parivartit hone kii ore bad rahaa he
 Modi indirectly targeted the Gandhi family and said, "corruption is destroying our country and those who are ruling the country, their families are submerged (in corruption)"
 jab tak ucchtam nyaayalay unhen fatkaar nahin lagaataa, ve lagaataar chuppi saadhe rahete hai or isamen jute rahete hai
 He said, therefore, brothers and sisters, the statement of Rashtrapati calls upon all of us to introspect and this concern should be at the top
 raashtrapati mukherjee ne buudhvaar ko kaha tha, bhrashtachar ek mukhya chunauti ban gaya he
 The priceless resources of the country are being destroyed due to kohli and apathy
 yah hamaare samaaj kii gatishiltaa ko kund kar rahe hai
 We need to stop this
 modi ne apane ghantabar ke bhaashan main sattarudh party dwaara sansad ko baadhit kiye jane kaa mudda bhi uthaaya
 "it can be understood in a democracy if the opposition parties raise their voice, but what is worrying is that for the first time in the country, the ruling party is not allowing the Lok Sabha to run and is hindering its functioning," he said
 modi ne kaha, unhone ise akhaada bana diya he or yadi aisa sattarudh party dwaara kiya jaataa he to sankat gaharaa ho jaataa he or isliye raashtrapati ji sansad ke kaamkaaj ke sambandh main aapke dwaara jataai gai chintaa vaastavik he
 He said in response to the President's concern about the disruption of Parliament, we should do our best to maintain the pride of Parliament, the temple of democracy
 modi ne apane bhaashan main pradhanmantri dwaara keval ek parivaar ko yaad karne or baaki sabhi anya mahaan netaaon ko bhuulane ke liye pradhanmantri par hamalaa bolaa or kaha, pradhanmantri ji, badi niraashaa kii baat he ki lalakile se aapane keval ek parivaar ke bare main bolaa
 Is it not better that today you should have remembered Sardar Vallabhbhai Patel, a person who united India, would it not have been better if a good message that united the country was given
 modi ne kaha, pradhanmantri ji, laal bahadur shastri, aapaki apni party ke pradhanmantri the

 vah bhi hamaare desh ke pradhanmantri rahe hai or unhone jai jawan, jai kisaan kaa naaraa diya tha

 aapako shastri ji kaa bhi naam lenaa chahie tha
 He said, no politics or politics of dynasty should have come in your way
 lekin aapane aisa kyon kiya

 i understand your compulsions, but why you did not remember the name of Lal Bahadur Shastriji
 
 
 
 i am not digesting this
 modi ne iske baad kaha, sardaar patel, jinhone puraa jivan congress kii seva main laga diya, aapako vah bhi yaad nahin rahe, is par hamen dil main pidaa hoti he
 Referring to the Food Security Bill and the letter written to the Prime Minister on this issue, Modi said, it would have been better if the Prime Minister had told the country
 tippaniyan He said, i have written a letter to the Prime Minister and suggested that there are many flaws in the Food Security Bill, which needs to be rectified
 hamane vidheyak kaa virodh nahin kiya he
 He said, we are not against serving food in the plate of the poor
 is vidheyak kii kamiyon ko sahi karnaa aapaki jimmedaari he, lekin aap (pradhanmantri) hamaari baat sunne ko taiyaar hi nahin hai
 Modi said, instead of serving food in the plate of poor people, this government is serving acid in the plate of poor people, sprinkling salt
 unhone kaha, khaadya suraksha vidheyak labhaarthiyon kii sankhya badhaane main vifal rahaa he, yah bhojan kii gunvattta badhaane main vifal rahaa he, yah bhojan kii keemat kam karne main vifal rahaa he
 
 
 And yet you are claiming that it is good for the people
 mukhyamantri modi ne kaha, is vidheyak ne jis tarah se hamaare sangheey dhaanche kii buniyaad kii andekhi kii he, main usase chintit hum
 It can get caught in some legal battles and poor people will again be deprived of food security
 unhone iske saath hi kaha, ham chaahate hai ki yah vidheyak ek acha vidheyak ho or iske liye maine pradhanmantri ko suzav diya tha ki vah sabhi mukhyamantriyon kii baithak bulaaen
 If you were concerned about the poor, you should have called a meeting and considered the shortcomings of the bill
 bhrashtachar par raashtrapati dwaara jataai gai chintaaon kaa zikr karte hue modi ne kaha, bharat ke raashtrapati ne bhrashtachar par apni gahari chintaa jaahir kii he
 He expressed his sorrow over it in his speech on Wednesday
 behatar hota ki lalakile se bhi bhrashtachar ke bare main kuch bolaa jaataa
 He said, the Prime Minister is your first right to respect the feelings and concerns of the President, but that has not happened today
 modi ne sawalia andaaj main kaha, ham bhrashtachar ke khilaaf yuddh kyon nahin ched sakate or
 
 
 Brothers and sisters
 
 
 is bhrashtachar kaa janm kahaan se hua he ?

 Modi said, in the old-fashioned television serials, nepotism was the main reason for corruption

 Until the Supreme Court reprimands them, they keep a constant silence and engage in it
 unhone kaha, isliye, bhaaiyon or bahanon, raashtrapatiji kaa bayaan ham sabhi se atmavlokan kaa aahvaan karata he or yah chintaa sheersh par honi chahie

 hamen ise rokane kii jarurat he

 unhone sansad main vyavdhaan ke sambandh main raashtrapati kii chintaa ke jawaab main kaha, hamen loktantr ke mandir, sansad kaa garv banaae rakhane main apni ore se behatar prayaas karnaa chahie

 On Thursday, Dimple Yadav, the Samajwadi Party (SP) leader and wife of Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav, who arrived in Kannauj to file nomination for the Lok Sabha elections, said that he was hopeful of winning again on Thursday, adding that he will continue to develop the district as before
 Will work pati akhilesh ke saath kannauj pahunchi dimple ne namakan dakhil karne se pehle ek jansabha ko sambodhit karte hue kaha ki kannauj ke logon ne hameshaa jati-dharm se upar uthakar samaajwaadiyon kaa saath diya he
 Dr
 ram manohar lohia se lekar mulaayam singh yadav or akhilesh yadav ko apana saansad chunaa he
 Dimple said that i sincerely hope that the people of Kannauj will elect me again and send me to Parliament
 main is baar bhi samarpit hokar pehle kii tarah jile ke vikaas kaa kaary karuungi
 In the 2012 by-election, the people here gave historical results without an election and sent me to the Parliament unopposed
 bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ke pradhanmantri pad ke ummidavaar narendra modi par nishaanaa sadhate hue dimple ne kaha ki kuch netaa lachchhedaar bhaashanon kaa sahaara le rahe hai, kyonki unhen dilli kii satta tak pahunchane ke liye koi or rasta nahin dikh rahaa he
 Describing this Lok Sabha election as very important, Dimple said that the country needs this time that Netaji (mulayam Singh Yadav) should become the Prime Minister
 unhone hameshaa sabko saath lekar chalane kaa kaam kiya he

 Badal Sarkar was born on July 5, 1925, one of the most eminent playwrights of India 
 bharat main naatak vidha par charchaa unke bina bemaani he
 Despite being written in original Bengali, dozens of his plays have been translated and played in other Indian languages with the same rigor
 hindi, angreji, marathi, gujarati, kannada, manipuri, asmi, punjabi bhaart or duniya kii anginat bhashaaon main unke naatak anudit hue or khele gaye
 Renowned art and literature critic Chinmay Guha had said, 'maybe a hundred years from now, there is a debate on whether in the twentieth and twenty-first century treaty period, there were three-three Badal governments at the same time, one of which was Saras But filled with intellectually intense dialogues, he kept his eye on the specifics of comic situations, wrote highly influential comedy dramas, others, which have shown world political tensions about violence in society Due to the dark shadow of war, of nuclear weapons, of terror, and of the growing economic inequality in society, he had recorded his voice in his plays and the third, who had captured the entertainment theater inside the auditoriums under a free speech to the general public
 'jawaharlal Nehru Fellowship, Padma Shri, awarded with Sangeet Natak Akademi Award and Sangeet Natak Akademi Fellowship
